border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">餐：含早餐、蒙古烤羊晚餐</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">宿：额尔古纳莉莉娅或同级别酒店</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(189, 66, 25);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">D4 style=\"font-size: 16px;\">秋季的呼伦贝尔，除了金色的森林与草原，道路两旁在秋季都是金色的草卷与麦田。我们在这里会享用一顿全部时蔬肉蛋都来自牧场自给的特色农家宴，坐着拖拉机驶向金色的白桦林，之后前往中国森林之都—— 根河</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">餐：含早餐、农场农家宴</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">宿：根河森林冰雪小镇或同级别酒店</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: - 海拉尔送机（合计车程约1.5H）</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">早餐后今天是我们的解散日，我们会统一安排一次送机至海拉尔机场，大家可以选择从海拉尔机场直接离开。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span
